should use a secondary wikipedia tag - linking to a broadcaster
linked wikidata entry (Q694837) is about a broadcaster, so it is very unlikely to be correct
subject:wikipedia=* or brand:wikipedia tag would be probably better (see https://wiki.openstreetmap.org/wiki/Key:wikipedia#Secondary_Wikipedia_links for full list of what else may be applicable)
in case of change remember to remove wikidata tag if it is present
object categorised by Wikidata - wrong classification may be caused by wrong data on Wikidata

no longer existing brand (according to Wikidata)
Wikidata claims that assigned brand object no longer exists. That means that either this shop is gone or it is rebranded. Or brand:wikidata tag is wrong. Historical, no longer existing object should not be mapped in OSM. REMEMBER TO VERIFY! WIKIDATA QUALITY MAY BE POOR! WIKIDATA MUST NOT BE USED AS SOURCE! ALWAYS VERIFY!

no longer existing object (according to Wikidata)
Wikidata claims that this object no longer exists. Historical, no longer existing object should not be mapped in OSM (except temporary marking to avoid remapping them from aerial imagery or similar sources) - so it means that either Wikidata is mistaken or has only partial data - for example it is fine to link ruins of a church to its wikipedia entry ( see https://www.wikidata.org/w/index.php?title=Wikidata:Project_chat&oldid=1361617968#Tagging_ruins/remains_left_after_object ) or wikipedia/wikidata tag is wrong or OSM has an outdated object that should be removed. REMEMBER TO VERIFY! WIKIDATA QUALITY MAY BE POOR! WIKIDATA MUST NOT BE USED AS SOURCE! ALWAYS VERIFY!
